#  Stendhal mapping file.
#  ---------------------
#   This file contains a set of lines that specify which correspondence exists between old tileset

#    
#    ../../zelda_outside_0_chipset.png:0:1:<new tileset file>:<position in the new tileset>
#    
#   You just need to worry about the first number after filename that is the position of the tile
#   in that image. You can get row and colum by doing row=(num/30) and column=(num mod 30)
#
#   Your help is really appreciated! :)
#   Regards,
#   Miguel
